***bakkeleien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bakkeleien.html>bakkeleien</a> (66011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ambonese_Malay" class="extiw" title="w:Ambonese Malay">Ambonese Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="abs">bakalai</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">berkelahi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bakkeleien.html>bakkeleien</a></strong>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:balans.html>balans</a> (4851)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">balanse</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:balance.html>balance</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bilanx</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balans.html>balans</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balansen.html>balansen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:balans.html>balansje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:balance.html>balance</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:scales.html>scales</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> weighing</li>
